je_rlg_start = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"
    
	is_shown_when_inactive = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 3  #3
			}
		}
	}

    possible = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 5 #5
			}
		}
	}
    
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_count
			value = 0
		}
	}
    
	complete = {
		exists = c:KOR
		this = c:KOR
		owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 10  #10
			}
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				level >= 10
			}
			has_building = building_railway
			state_population > 3000000
		}
		OR = {
			#exists = c:USA
			#exists = c:USA
			#exists = c:USA
			#exists = c:USA
			#exists = c:USA
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				type = increase_relations
				who = c:USA
			}
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				type = increase_relations
				who = c:AUS
			}
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				type = increase_relations
				who = c:PRU
			}
			#has_diplomatic_pact = {
			#    type = increase_relations
			#    who = c:GER
			#}
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				type = increase_relations
				who = c:GBR
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = je_rlg_start_deci
			has_variable = lia_var_rlg_start
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = lia_event_rlg.1
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_metropolis
		}
	}

	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	#should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}

je_rlg_metropolis = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
			value = 0
		}
	}

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		#trigger_event = {
		#	id = lia_event_rlg.1
		#}
        custom_tooltip = {
            text = je_rlg_metropolis_clear
        }
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_2
        hidden_effect = {
            every_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_WONSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                }
            }
            every_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                }
            }
        }
        
	}
    
	#on_weekly_pulse = {
	#	effect = {
	#	}
	#}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 3
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	#should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}
je_rlg_rural_exodus = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

	is_shown_when_inactive = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        exists = var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis
        var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis >= 1
	}

    possible = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        exists = var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis
        custom_tooltip = {
            text = je_rlg_metropolis_goal
            var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis >= 3
        }
	}

	immediate = {
	}

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
        custom_tooltip = {
            text = je_rlg_rural_exodus_clear
        }
        set_variable = lia_var_rlg_add_3
        hidden_effect = {
            every_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_UIJU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_WONSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_ULSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_DAEJEON
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU
                        state_region = s:STATE_LIA_JEJU
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_1
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_2
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_gocity_3
                }
            }
            every_scope_state = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_SEOUL
                        state_region = s:STATE_PYONGYANG
                        state_region = s:STATE_SARIWON
                        state_region = s:STATE_BUSAN
                        state_region = s:STATE_YANGHO
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_1
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_2
                remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                add_modifier = {
                    name = lia_rlg_modi_outrural_3
                }
            }
        }
        
	}
    
	#on_weekly_pulse = {
	#	effect = {
	#	}
	#}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_metropolis
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 5
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	#should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}
####이건 그냥 제안인데, 나중에 항만임대계약 기능을 만드는걸 한번 생각해봐. 내가 또 까먹을까봐 여따가 적어둠.
je_rlg_seoul_1 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_1_con1
                    state_population > 500000
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_railway
                    level >= 5
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_government_administration
                    level >= 10
                }
                has_decree = decree_greener_grass_campaign
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_1_con2
                    state_unemployment_rate < 0.05
                }
            }
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
			value = 0
		}
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_count
            add = 1
        }
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_seoul_2
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_1
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_2
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.100
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.101
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.102
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.103
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.104
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.108
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.109
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.100
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_railway
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.101
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_government_administration
                                level >= 10
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.102
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            has_decree = decree_greener_grass_campaign
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.103
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_unemployment_rate < 0.05
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.104
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_seoul_1
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}
je_rlg_seoul_2 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR

		s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
            region_state:KOR = {

                    text = je_rlg_seoul_2_con1
                    state_population > 1000000
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_barracks
                    level >= 5
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_power_plant
                    level >= 5
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_2_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 1000
                }
            }
        }

		}
        trigger_event = {
            id = lia_event_rlg.114
            days = { 30 360 }
        }
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_seoul_3
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_2

                name = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_3

                id = lia_event_rlg.113
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
            add = 1
        }
        trigger_event = {

	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59

		#}

je_rlg_seoul_3 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_3_con1
                    state_population > 2000000
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_university
                    level >= 10
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_3_con3
                    AND = {
                        any_scope_pop = {
                            has_pop_culture = korean
                        }
                        any_scope_pop = {
                            has_pop_culture = han
                        }
                        any_scope_pop = {
                            has_pop_culture = japanese
                        }
                    }
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_seoul_3_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 2000
                }
            }
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_3
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_seoul_4
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_3
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_seoul_metro_4
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.120
            }

        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금

		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.129
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 2000000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.120
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_university
                                level >= 10
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.121
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            AND = {
                                any_scope_pop = {
                                    has_pop_culture = korean
                                }
                                any_scope_pop = {
                                    has_pop_culture = han
                                }
                                any_scope_pop = {
                                    has_pop_culture = japanese
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.122
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 2000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.123
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_3
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_3
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_seoul_3
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_seoul_3

		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_incheon_a_4
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_3
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_a_4
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {

            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.221
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.222
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.223
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.228
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.229
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 1000000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.220
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_port
                                level >= 7
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.221
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_free_trade
                        has_law = law_type:law_protectionism
                        has_law = law_type:law_mercantilism
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.222
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 1000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.223
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_a_3
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_a_3
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_a_3
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_incheon_a_3
	}

		add = 256
	}

je_rlg_incheon_b_3 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
		s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_incheon_b_3_con1
                    state_population > 1000000
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_food_industry
                    level >= 5
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_incheon_b_3_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 1000
                }
            }
        }
        AND = {
            has_technology_researched = organized_sports
            has_technology_researched = camera
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_b_3
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_incheon_b_4
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_3
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_incheon_b_4
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.270
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.271
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.272
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.273
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.278
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.279
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 1000000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.270
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    AND = {
                        has_technology_researched = organized_sports
                        has_technology_researched = camera
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.271
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_food_industry
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.272
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_INCHEON = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 1000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.273
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_b_3
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_b_3
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_incheon_b_3
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_incheon_b_3
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}

            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.460
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_railway
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.461
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_pop = {
                                is_pop_type = soldiers
                                standard_of_living >= 14
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.462
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_KAESONG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.463
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_kaesong_b_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_kaesong_b_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_kaesong_b_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금

		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.519
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.510
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_port
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.511
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_shipyards
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.512
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.513
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_a_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_a_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_a_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}

                name = lia_rlg_modi_nampho_b_3
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.560
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.561
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.562
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.563
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
            add = 1
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.568
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.569
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.560
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_PYONGYANG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_lead_mine
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.561
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_steel_mills
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.562
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAMPHO = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.563
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_b_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_b_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_nampho_b_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_nampho_b_2
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}

je_rlg_uiju_a_2 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_PYONGYANG
		s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_2_con1
                    state_population > 750000
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_2_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 750
                }
            }
        }
        AND = {
            NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SHENGJING }
            NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BEIJING }
            custom_tooltip = {
                text = je_rlg_uiju_a_2_con3
                scaled_debt < 0.01
            }
        }
        custom_tooltip = {
            text = je_rlg_uiju_a_2_con4
            any_country = {
                s:STATE_BEIJING = {
                    any_scope_state = {
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_building_type = building_railway
                            level >= 1
                        }
                        percent >= 1.00
                    }
                }
                s:STATE_SHENGJING = {
                    any_scope_state = {
                        any_scope_building = {
                            is_building_type = building_railway
                            level >= 1
                        }
                        percent >= 1.00
                    }
                }
            }
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_2
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_uiju_a_3
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_UIJU.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_uiju_a_2
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_uiju_a_3
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.610
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.611
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.612
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.613
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
            add = 1
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.618
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.619
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.610
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    AND = {
                        NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SHENGJING }
                        NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BEIJING }
                        scaled_debt < 0.01
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.611
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    AND = {
                        s:STATE_BEIJING = {
                            any_scope_state = {
                                any_scope_building = {
                                    is_building_type = building_railway
                                    level >= 1
                                }
                                percent >= 1.00
                            }
                        }
                        s:STATE_SHENGJING = {
                            any_scope_state = {
                                any_scope_building = {
                                    is_building_type = building_railway
                                    level >= 1
                                }
                                percent >= 1.00
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.612
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.613
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_2
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}
je_rlg_uiju_a_3 = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_PYONGYANG
		s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_3_con1
                    state_population > 1000000
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_3_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 1000
                }
            }
        }
        AND = {
            investment_pool >= 1000000
            has_technology_researched = mutual_funds
        }
		s:STATE_PYONGYANG = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_power_plant
                    level >= 10
                }
            }
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_3
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_uiju_a_4
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_UIJU.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_uiju_a_3
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_uiju_a_4
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.

                id = lia_event_rlg.620
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.621
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.622
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.623
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.628
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.629
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 1000000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.620
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    AND = {
                        investment_pool >= 1000000
                        has_technology_researched = mutual_funds
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.621
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_PYONGYANG = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_power_plant
                                level >= 10
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.622
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_UIJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 1000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.623
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_3
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic

                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_4_con3
                    any_scope_pop = {
                        strata = rich
                        standard_of_living >= 40
                    }

                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_paper_mills
                    level >= 5
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_uiju_a_4_con2

                }
            }
        }
		s:STATE_PYONGYANG = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_logging_camp
                    level >= 10
                }
            }
        }
        has_technology_researched = international_exchange_standards
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_uiju_a_4

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.53
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.54
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.55
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.56
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.57
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.58
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.59

		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.709
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.700
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_port
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.701
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_unemployment_rate < 0.05
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.702
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 500
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.703
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_1
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_1
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_1
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}

            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_najin_a_5
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.730
            }
            trigger_event = {

            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.732
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.733
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.50 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.51
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.52

		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.739
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 1500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.730
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_MOSCOW }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_TVER }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_GALICH }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_PERM }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_URAL }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_TOBOLSK }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_TOMSK }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_IRKUTSK }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_TRANS_BAIKAL }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_OKHOTSK }
                    NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_OUTER_MANCHURIA }
					NOT = { owns_entire_state_region = STATE_EAFP_OUTER_MANCHURIA }	#외만주 쪼개기로 인한 주 추가!
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_MOSCOW
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_TVER
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_GALICH
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_PERM
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }

                        state_region = s:STATE_URAL
                        has_building = building_railway

                        state_region = s:STATE_TOBOLSK
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_TOMSK
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_IRKUTSK
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_TRANS_BAIKAL
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_OKHOTSK
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {
                        state_region = s:STATE_OUTER_MANCHURIA
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                    any_state = {	#외만주 쪼개기로 인한 주 추가!
                        state_region = s:STATE_EAFP_OUTER_MANCHURIA
                        has_building = building_railway
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.731
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_technology_researched = international_exchange_standards
                    any_country = {
                        has_state_in_state_region = STATE_BEIJING
                        #any_scope_state = {
                        #    state_region = s:STATE_BEIJING
                        #}
                        relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
                    }
                    any_country = {
                        has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MOSCOW
                        #any_scope_state = {
                        #    state_region = s:STATE_MOSCOW
                        #}
                        relations:root >= relations_threshold:cordial
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.732
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_NAJIN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 1500
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.733
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_4
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_4
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_najin_a_4
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_najin_a_4
	}

		add = 256

		#	120 = 0

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.82

		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.829
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {

                            state_population > 1000000
                        }
                    }
                }

                    id = lia_event_rlg.820

                            }
                        }
                    }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도

                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting

                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic

		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_busan_a_3
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_busan_a_2
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_busan_a_3
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.910
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.911
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.912
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.913
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
            add = 1
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.90 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.91
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.92
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.93
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.94
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.95
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.96
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.97
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.98
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.99
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.918
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.919
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.910
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_port
                                level >= 5
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_mercantilism
                        has_law = law_type:law_protectionism
                        has_law = law_type:law_free_trade
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_no_migration_controls
                        has_law = law_type:law_migration_controls
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.911
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_shipyards
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.912
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.913
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_a_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_a_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_a_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_busan_a_2
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
