	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_map.dds"

    complete = {
        exists = c:KOR
        this = c:KOR
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_BUSAN
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SEOUL
        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
		s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_busan_b_2_con1
                    state_population > 750000
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_naval_base
                    level >= 10
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_port
                    level >= 3
                }
                any_scope_building = {
                    is_building_type = building_shipyards
                    level >= 3
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_busan_b_2_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 750
                }
            }
        }
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_busan_b_2
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_rlg_busan_b_3
		}
        s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_busan_b_2
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_busan_b_3
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.960
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.961
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.962
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.963
            }
        }
        change_variable = {
            name = lia_var_rlg_metropolis
            add = 1
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.90 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.91
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.92
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.93
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.94
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.95
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.96
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.97
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.98
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.99
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.968
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.969
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 750000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.960
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_naval_base
                                level >= 10
                            }
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_shipyards
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.961
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_port
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.962
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_BUSAN = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 750
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.963
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_b_2
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_b_2
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_busan_b_2
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_busan_b_2
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}

                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                }

                }

                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }

                }
            }

                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic

                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }

                change_variable = {

                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic

                    }

                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting

                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting

                change_variable = {

                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_ulsan_b_1
                    add = 2

            }
		}

        s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_daegu_a_1
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_daegu_a_2
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1100
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1101
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1102
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1103
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.110 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.111
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.112
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.113
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.114
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.115
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.116
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.117
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.118
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.119
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1108
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1109
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1100
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_railway
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1101
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_unemployment_rate < 0.05
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1102
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 500
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1103
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_daegu_a_1
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_daegu_a_1
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_daegu_a_1
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_daegu_a_1
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes

        }

                id = lia_event_rlg.1152
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1153
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.110 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.111
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.112
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.113
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.114
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.115

		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.117
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.118
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.119
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1158
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1159
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1150
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_DAEGU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_railway
                                level >= 3
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1151
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1153
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_daegu_b_1
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {

                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_daegu_b_1
                    add = 2

        owns_entire_state_region = STATE_YANGHO
		s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
            region_state:KOR = {
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_gwangju_a_4_con1
                    state_population > 1500000
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_gwangju_a_4_con3
                    any_scope_pop = {
                        strata = poor
                        standard_of_living >= 16
                    }
                }
                custom_tooltip = {
                    text = je_rlg_gwangju_a_4_con2
                    total_urbanization >= 1500
                }
            }
        }
        has_technology_researched = film
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_gwangju_a_4
			value = 0
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
        s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU.region_state:KOR = {
            remove_modifier = lia_rlg_modi_gwangju_a_4
            add_modifier = {
                name = lia_rlg_modi_gwangju_a_5
            }
        }
        hidden_effect = {   #저널목표 달성이벤트 출력 체크는 한달마다지만 저널 깨지는건 바로니까, 혹시라도 놓친 이벤트 있으면 보고 넘어가도록 하는 조치.
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1330
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1331
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1332
            }
            trigger_event = {
                id = lia_event_rlg.1333
            }
        }
	}
    
    on_monthly_pulse = {
		#random_events = {  확률 3 이하는 전 도시개발 컨텐츠 저널퀘 공통이벤트, 확률 5이상 이벤트는 해당 저널퀘 고유 이벤트
		#	120 = 0
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.130 국고보조금
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.131
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.132
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.133
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.134
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.135
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.136
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.137
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.138
		#	2 = lia_event_rlg.139
        
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1338
		#	5 = lia_event_rlg.1339
		#}

        effect = {
            if = {  #목표별 달성시 이벤트
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            state_population > 1500000
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1330
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            any_scope_pop = {
                                strata = poor
                                standard_of_living >= 16
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1331
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_technology_researched = film
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1332
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    s:STATE_LIA_GWANGJU = {
                        region_state:KOR = {
                            total_urbanization >= 1500
                        }
                    }
                }
                trigger_event = {
                    id = lia_event_rlg.1333
                    days = { 1 7 }
                }
            }

            if = {  #정부체제별 기본진행도
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_census_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_universal_suffrage
                        has_law = law_type:law_anarchy
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_gwangju_a_4
                    add = 4
                }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic
                        has_law = law_type:law_council_republic
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_autocracy
                        has_law = law_type:law_oligarchy
                        has_law = law_type:law_landed_voting
                        has_law = law_type:law_wealth_voting
                    }
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_gwangju_a_4
                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_gwangju_a_4
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_gwangju_a_4
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 256
	}
    
	progressbar = yes
    
	#fail = {
	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	should_be_pinned_by_default = yes
}

                    }

                    add = 3
                }
            }
            else = {
                change_variable = {
                    name = lia_var_rlg_jeju_b_3
                    add = 2
                }
            }
		}
	}

		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_jeju_b_3

		add = 256

je_rlg_seoul_gyeongbokgung_rebuild = {
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_industry.dds"

	complete = {
		exists = c:KOR
		this = c:KOR
		owns_entire_state_region = STATE_LIA_SEOUL
		s:STATE_LIA_SEOUL = {
			region_state:KOR = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_gyeongbokgung_poor
				}
			}
		}
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
	}
	
	scripted_button = lia_eafp_scripted_button_wonnap
	scripted_button = lia_eafp_scripted_button_dangbaek

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = lia_var_rlg_wonnap_possible
		trigger_event = {
			id = lia_event_rlg.1500
		}
	}

	on_complete = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = lia_event_rlg.1510
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dangbaek
			}
			remove_building = building_dangbaek
		}
	}
	
	on_weekly_pulse = {
		random_events = {
			100 = 0
			10 = lia_event_rlg.1504	#화재
			10 = lia_event_rlg.1507	#상소
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild >= 500
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = lia_event_rlg.1504
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_monthly_pulse = {
		effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_gyeongbokgung_poor
							has_active_production_method = pm_rebuild_gyeongbokgung_1
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
						add = 20
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_gyeongbokgung_poor
							has_active_production_method = pm_rebuild_gyeongbokgung_2
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
						add = 30
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_gyeongbokgung_poor
							has_active_production_method = pm_rebuild_gyeongbokgung_3
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
						add = 40
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_gyeongbokgung_poor
							has_active_production_method = pm_rebuild_gyeongbokgung_4
						}
					}
					change_variable = {
						name = lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
						add = 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
    
	current_value = {
		value = root.var:lia_var_rlg_gyeongbokgung_rebuild
	}

	goal_add_value = {
		add = 1000
	}
    
	progressbar = yes

	#}

	#on_fail = {
	#}
    
	#invalid = {
	#}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fire.dds"

	complete = {
		scope:journal_entry = {
			is_goal_complete = yes
		}
		always = no
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = lia_var_rlg_dangbaek_inflation
			value = 0
		}
	}
	
	timeout = 1460

	on_timeout = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dangbaek
			}
			remove_building = building_dangbaek
		}
	}
	
	on_complete = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = lia_event_rlg.1509
		}
	}
	
	fail = {
		NOT = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_dangbaek
			}
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dangbaek
			}
			remove_building = building_dangbaek
		}
	}
	
	on_weekly_pulse = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:lia_var_rlg_dangbaek_inflation <= 100
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_dangbaek
						has_active_production_method = pm_base_dangbaek_1

					name = lia_var_rlg_dangbaek_inflation

						has_active_production_method = pm_base_dangbaek_2

					name = lia_var_rlg_dangbaek_inflation
					subtract = 1.5
